We request you to kindly take the above information on record.

Pursuant to Section 108 of the Companies Act, 2013 read with Rule 20 of the Companies (Management and Administration) Rules, 2014, we are attaching details of Voting Results of remote e-voting and e-voting at the AGM as required under Regulation 44 (3) of the SEBI (LODR) Regulations, 2015 in respect of the resolutions set out in the Notice of 35th Annual General Meeting (AGM) held through Video Conference on Tuesday, the 15th December 2020 at 04:00 pm (IST) at the Registered Office of the Company.We are also attaching herewith Combined Report of remote e-voting and e-voting at the AGM for each Resolution, issued by CS Shalin Patel, Scrutinizer. Kindly take the above on records and acknowledge the receipt.
